<p><b>Joshua Walter Kimmich</b> (<small>German pronunciation:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Standard_German" title="Help:IPA/Standard German">[jozua kmç]</a></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> born 8 February 1995) is a German professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defensive_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Defensive midfielder">defensive midfielder</a> or <a href="/wiki/Right-back" class="mw-redirect" title="Right-back">right-back</a> for <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> club <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany national team</a>. 
</p><p>Known for his versatility, passing, shooting, tackling and aggression, Kimmich is considered as both one of the best midfielders and right backs in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He is often compared with former Bayern Munich captain <a href="/wiki/Philipp_Lahm" title="Philipp Lahm">Philipp Lahm</a> and is considered his successor.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kimmich joined Bayern Munich from <a href="/wiki/RB_Leipzig" title="RB Leipzig">RB Leipzig</a> in 2015 for contract lasting until 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> In the 2019–20 season, after winning the continental treble with Bayern Munich, Kimmich was included in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a>, the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World_XI" title="FIFPro">FIFA FIFPro Men's World11</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> and was recognized as the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Club_Football_Awards#Men&#39;s_award_2" title="UEFA Club Football Awards">UEFA Champions League Defender of the Season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kimmich played youth football for <a href="/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a>.
</p><p>He then went on to join <a href="/wiki/RB_Leipzig" title="RB Leipzig">RB Leipzig</a> in July 2013. Stuttgart secured an option to rebuy.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He made his <a href="/wiki/3._Liga" title="3. Liga">3. Liga</a> debut for the club on 28 September of that year, as a substitute for <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Rockenbach" title="Thiago Rockenbach">Thiago Rockenbach</a> in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/SpVgg_Unterhaching" title="SpVgg Unterhaching">SpVgg Unterhaching</a>. He scored his first professional goal in a 3–2 victory over <a href="/wiki/1._FC_Saarbr%C3%BCcken" title="1. FC Saarbrücken">1. FC Saarbrücken</a> on 30 November 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_RB_Leipzig_season" title="2013–14 RB Leipzig season">2013–14 season</a> with one goal in 26 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-2013–14_season_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013–14_season-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kimmich scored his first goal of the season in a 3–2 victory against <a href="/wiki/1._FC_Union_Berlin" title="1. FC Union Berlin">Union Berlin</a> on 1 March 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_RB_Leipzig_season" title="2014–15 RB Leipzig season">2014–15 season</a> with two goals in 29 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-2014–15_season_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2014–15_season-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kimmich left the club with a tally of three goals in fifty three league appearances for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bayern_Munich">Bayern Munich</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Bayern Munich">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9317"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–17">2015–17</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 2015–17">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 2 January 2015, Kimmich agreed to join <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> on a five-year contract lasting until 30 June 2020, for a reported fee of €7 million, most of which went to VfB Stuttgart.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut for the club on 9 August, starting in the first round of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_DFB-Pokal" title="2015–16 DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_N%C3%B6ttingen" title="FC Nöttingen">FC Nöttingen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> gave him his <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> debut the following month on 12 September when he entered play as a late substitute at home against <a href="/wiki/FC_Augsburg" title="FC Augsburg">FC Augsburg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, Kimmich made his first appearance in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> in Bayern's tournament opener away at <a href="/wiki/Olympiacos_F.C." title="Olympiacos F.C.">Olympiakos</a> and he started in the Bundesliga for the first time three days thereafter, playing 90 minutes against <a href="/wiki/SV_Darmstadt_98" title="SV Darmstadt 98">SV Darmstadt 98</a> in a 3–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kimmich ended his first season at Bayern having made 23 league appearances of which 15 were starts.<sup id="cite_ref-2015–16_season_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2015–16_season-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He also played the full 120 minutes in Bayern's <a href="/wiki/2016_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2016 DFB-Pokal Final">2016 DFB-Pokal Final</a> defeat of <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_(Berlin)" title="Olympiastadion (Berlin)">Berlin Olympiastadion</a> on 21 May.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg/220px-Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="305" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg/330px-Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg/440px-Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2772" data-file-height="3843" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Joshua_Kimmich_Training_2017-03_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kimmich during training with Bayern Munich, 2017</div></div></div>
<p>Kimmich started the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2016–17 FC Bayern Munich season">2016–17 season</a> by coming on as a substitute in a 2–0 win against Borussia Dortmund in the <a href="/wiki/2016_DFL-Supercup" title="2016 DFL-Supercup">2016 DFL-Supercup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Im_zweiten_Anlauf:_Vidal_beschert_Bayern_den_ersten_Titel_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Im_zweiten_Anlauf:_Vidal_beschert_Bayern_den_ersten_Titel-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> On 9 September, he scored his first goal for FC Bayern in a 2–0 <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Bundesliga" title="2016–17 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a>, away win at <a href="/wiki/FC_Schalke_04" title="FC Schalke 04">FC Schalke 04</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he scored his first two <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> goals in a 5–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/FC_Rostov" title="FC Rostov">FC Rostov</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Kimmich scored a late winning goal in the 88th minute in a 1–0 away victory over <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> He finished the 2016–17 season with nine goals in forty appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-Im_zweiten_Anlauf:_Vidal_beschert_Bayern_den_ersten_Titel_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Im_zweiten_Anlauf:_Vidal_beschert_Bayern_den_ersten_Titel-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2016–17_season_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2016–17_season-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9320"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–20">2017–20</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2017–20">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kimmich played in the <a href="/wiki/2017_DFL-Supercup" title="2017 DFL-Supercup">2017 DFL-Supercup</a> and won the title as Bayern defeated their arch-rival Borussia Dortmund on 5–4 penalties after the <a href="/wiki/Overtime_(sports)" title="Overtime (sports)">extra time</a> ended 2–2.<sup id="cite_ref-Bayerns_erster_Titel_dank_Flippertor_und_Ulreich_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bayerns_erster_Titel_dank_Flippertor_und_Ulreich-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> On 16 September, he provided overall three assists to <a href="/wiki/Thomas_M%C3%BCller" title="Thomas Müller">Thomas Müller</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arjen_Robben" title="Arjen Robben">Arjen Robben</a> and <a href="/wiki/Robert_Lewandowski" title="Robert Lewandowski">Robert Lewandowski</a>'s goals to defeat <a href="/wiki/1._FSV_Mainz_05" title="1. FSV Mainz 05">1. FSV Mainz 05</a> with a 4–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> On 9 March 2018, Kimmich signed a three-year contract extension which lasts until 30 June 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> He managed to score each goal in both the first and second leg in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League semi-final</a> tie against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>, but his side were knocked out from the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">competition</a> on 4–3 <a href="/wiki/Two-legged_tie" title="Two-legged tie">aggregate</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Kimmich finished the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2017–18 FC Bayern Munich season">2017–18 season</a> with six goals and seventeen assists in 47 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-2017–18_season_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017–18_season-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 August, Kimmich started the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2018–19 FC Bayern Munich season">2018–19 season</a> by playing in the <a href="/wiki/2018_DFL-Supercup" title="2018 DFL-Supercup">German Super Cup</a> and also won the title as his side defeated <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a> with a 5–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-FCB_gewinnt_Supercup_-_Lewandowski_macht_den_Unterschied_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FCB_gewinnt_Supercup_-_Lewandowski_macht_den_Unterschied-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> The following week, on 18 August 2018, Kimmich played in the 1–0 win against <a href="/wiki/SV_Drochtersen/Assel" title="SV Drochtersen/Assel">SV Drochtersen/Assel</a> in the first round of the German Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Kimmich played in the opening match of the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Bundesliga" title="2018–19 Bundesliga">Bundesliga season</a> against <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">1899 Hoffenheim</a> on 24 August 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-Ereignisreiche_Schlussphase:_Bayern_gewinnt_Eröffnungsspiel_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ereignisreiche_Schlussphase:_Bayern_gewinnt_Eröffnungsspiel-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Bayern won the match 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-Ereignisreiche_Schlussphase:_Bayern_gewinnt_Eröffnungsspiel_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ereignisreiche_Schlussphase:_Bayern_gewinnt_Eröffnungsspiel-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Kimmich's first goal of the season came against <a href="/wiki/Hannover_96" title="Hannover 96">Hannover 96</a> on 15 December 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> He made his 100th league appearance for the club on 9 February 2019 during a 3–1 win over rivals, Schalke.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kimmich played every single minute in all 34 matches in the Bundesliga. In those 34 matches, Kimmich scored two goals and finished second in the league with 13 assists.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On 14 August 2020, Kimmich scored one goal and provided an assist in an <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona_2%E2%80%938_FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Barcelona 2–8 FC Bayern Munich">8–2</a> win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2019–20 UEFA Champions League">2019–20 UEFA Champions League</a> quarter-final.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> On 23 August 2020, Kimmich made an important assist for the winning goal against <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> by <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Coman" title="Kingsley Coman">Kingsley Coman</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2020 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> to be his first Champions League title along with his teammate <a href="/wiki/Serge_Gnabry" title="Serge Gnabry">Serge Gnabry</a>, another VfB Stuttgart academy product.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kimmich started the 2020–21 season by acquiring the number 6 shirt, after <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Alc%C3%A2ntara" title="Thiago Alcântara">Thiago Alcântara</a> who had worn it for seven years departed for <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> On 30 September 2020, he scored the winning goal in a 3–2 win over Borussia Dortmund in the <a href="/wiki/2020_DFL-Supercup" title="2020 DFL-Supercup">2020 DFL-Supercup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On 27 October, Kimmich scored the winning goal in a 2–1 away victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Lokomotiv_Moscow" title="FC Lokomotiv Moscow">Lokomotiv Moscow</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">2020–21 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimmich2014.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Kimmich2014.jpg/220px-Kimmich2014.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Kimmich2014.jpg/330px-Kimmich2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Kimmich2014.jpg/440px-Kimmich2014.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimmich2014.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kimmich playing for Germany's youth squad in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 17 May 2016, Kimmich was named in <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>'s preliminary 27-man squad for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 31 May 2016, he was named in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_squads#Germany" title="UEFA Euro 2016 squads">final 23-man squad</a> and given the shirt number 21.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 21 June 2016, Kimmich was selected to start for Germany in their final <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_Group_C" title="UEFA Euro 2016 Group C">Group C</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Northern Ireland national football team">Northern Ireland</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/Benedikt_H%C3%B6wedes" title="Benedikt Höwedes">Benedikt Höwedes</a> at right-back.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Kimmich remained Germany's first-choice right-back as they reached the semi-finals and was named in UEFA's Team of the Tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-UEFA_2016_TotT_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFA_2016_TotT-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 September 2016, Kimmich scored his first goal for the German national team in a 3–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Norway_national_football_team" title="Norway national football team">Norway</a> during <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 May 2017, Kimmich was included in <a href="/wiki/Joachim_L%C3%B6w" title="Joachim Löw">Joachim Löw</a>'s Germany <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_squads#Germany" title="2017 FIFA Confederations Cup squads">squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2017 FIFA Confederations Cup">2017 FIFA Confederations Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> He started in all five of the team's matches at the tournament, registering two assists, as Germany won its first Confederations Cup title.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>On 6 June 2017, Kimmich scored from a stunning overhead kick in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Denmark_national_football_team" title="Denmark national football team">Denmark</a> in the 88th minute of the game which helped Germany to grab their late equaliser against Denmark, as the match ended up 1–1.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 June 2018, Kimmich was selected for Germany's final <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads#Germany" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">23-man squad</a> by Joachim Löw for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 17 June 2018, Kimmich made his <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">World Cup</a> debut against <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a> in their opening match, but the game ended in a 1–0 loss for Germany.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 September 2018, Kimmich started Germany's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Nations_League" title="UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a> opener against <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>, playing as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a> for the first time in 18 months.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/Horst_Hrubesch" title="Horst Hrubesch">Horst Hrubesch</a> has praised Kimmich for his versatility, saying "Joshua has enormous quality and is versatile in both attacking and defensive roles". Remarking on Kimmich's versatility, a 2017 article on the Bundesliga's official website referred to him as a "veritable <a href="/wiki/Swiss_Army_knife" title="Swiss Army knife">Swiss Army knife</a> of a player", citing Guardiola's conversion of a player he once referred to as "one of the best defensive midfielder in the world" into a right-back.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Amin_Younes" title="Amin Younes">Amin Younes</a> complimented Kimmich's defensive awareness as well in an interview, after the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="UEFA European Under-21 Championship">U21 EURO</a> group stage. "Winning the ball back superbly. He does that really well", Younes told to the media. During the U21 competition, Philip Röber of <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a>.com, described Kimmich's playing style on the website and compared him to <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0lkay_G%C3%BCndo%C4%9Fan" title="lkay Gündoan">lkay Gündoan</a>, but other critics compared him to retired Bayern captain <a href="/wiki/Philipp_Lahm" title="Philipp Lahm">Philipp Lahm</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WK_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WK-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup></p><blockquote><p>At Leipzig, he was part of an extremely attack-minded team in which his ball-winning qualities in front of a high back four shone through. In the Germany U21 side, he has a deeper role, but he has also caught the eye as a tidy defensive midfielder. Kimmich has great timing in his tackles, can dribble and does not mind putting in the legwork.</p></blockquote>
<p>Kimmich himself has cited <a href="/wiki/Bastian_Schweinsteiger" title="Bastian Schweinsteiger">Bastian Schweinsteiger</a> as his inspiration.<sup id="cite_ref-WK_65-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WK-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joshua_Kimmich&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kimmich has two children, a son, born in 2019,<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> and a daughter, born in October 2020, with his girlfriend Lina Meyer.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He launched an online initiative "We Kick Corona" with his Bayern Munich teammate <a href="/wiki/Leon_Goretzka" title="Leon Goretzka">Leon Goretzka</a>, to help charitable, social or medical institutions during the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

	<h3 id="p-personal-label" class="vector-menu-heading">
		<span>Personal tools</span>
